Vertex shader: ../p5/gouraud.vert

  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |struct LightSource {
 12 |  vec4 ambient, diffuse, specular;
 13 |  vec4 positionWorld;
 14 |  vec4 positionEye;
 15 |  vec3 spotDirectionWorld;
 16 |  int directional;
 17 |  vec3 spotDirectionEye;
 18 |  int enabled;
 19 |  float spotExponent, spotCutoff, spotCosCutoff;
 20 |  vec3 attenuation;
 21 |};
 22 |layout (std140, binding=2) uniform Lights {
 23 |  LightSource lights[4];
 24 |};
 25 |layout (std140, binding=1) uniform Material {
 26 |vec4 diffuse;
 27 |vec4 ambient;
 28 |vec4 specular;
 29 |vec4 emissive;
 30 |float shininess;
 31 |int textureCount;
 32 |};
 33 |
 34 |uint numDiffTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 0, 3); }
 35 |uint numSpecTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 3, 3); }
 36 |uint numNormTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 6, 3); }
 37 |uint numHeightTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 9, 3); }
 38 |uint numOpacTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 12, 3); }
 39 |uint numAmbTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 15, 3); }
 40 |
 41 |in vec4 position;
 42 |in vec3 normal;
 43 |
 44 |out vec4 color;
 45 |
 46 |// Suponiendo fuentes puntuales
 47 |vec4 iluminacion(vec3 pos, vec3 N, vec3 V) {
 48 |  // Componente emisiva del material
 49 |  vec4 color = emissive;
 50 |  for (int i = 0; i < lights.length(); i++) {
 51 |    // Si la fuente est apagada, no tenerla en cuenta
 52 |    if (lights[i].enabled == 0)
 53 |      continue;
 54 |
 55 |    // Vector iluminacin (desde vrtice a la fuente)
 56 |    vec3 L = normalize(vec3(lights[i].positionEye) - pos);
 57 |
 58 |    // Multiplicador de la componente difusa
 59 |    float diffuseMult = max(dot(N, L), 0.0);
 60 |    float specularMult = 0.0;
 61 |    if (diffuseMult > 0.0) {
 62 |      // Multiplicador de la componente especular
 63 |      vec3 R = reflect(-L, N);
 64 |      specularMult = max(0.0, dot(R, V));
 65 |      specularMult = pow(specularMult, shininess);
 66 |    }
 67 |
 68 |    float d = distance(pos, vec3(lights[i].positionEye));
 69 |    float attenuation_factor = 1.0/max(1, 
 70 |        attenuation.x + attenuation.y*d + attenuation.z*pow(d,2));
 71 |
 72 |    float efecto_foco = 0;
 73 |
 74 |    color += attenuation_factor * (lights[i].ambient * ambient +
 75 |             lights[i].diffuse * diffuse * diffuseMult +
 76 |             lights[i].specular * specular * specularMult);
 77 |  }
 78 |
 79 |  return color;
 80 |}
 81 |
 82 |void main() {
 83 |  // Normal en el espacio de la cmara
 84 |  vec3 eN = normalize(normalMatrix * normal);
 85 |  // Vrtice en el espacio de la cmara
 86 |  vec3 eposition = vec3(modelviewMatrix * position);
 87 |  // Vector vista (desde vrtice a la cmara)
 88 |  vec3 V = normalize(-eposition.xyz);
 89 |  // Clculo de la iluminacin
 90 |  color = iluminacion(eposition, eN, V);
 91 |  gl_Position = modelviewprojMatrix * position;
 92 |}
 93 |

[Fri Apr 29 18:44:11 2022] INF: [shader.cpp (169)] Compilando ../p5/gouraud.vert
[Fri Apr 29 18:44:11 2022] ERR: [program.cpp (223)] Error compilando el shader:0(75) : error C1503: undefined variable "spotDirection"
0(76) : error C1503: undefined variable "spotCutoff"
0(79) : error C1503: undefined variable "spotCosCutoff"
0(83) : error C1503: undefined variable "spotExponent"

Vertex shader: ../p5/gouraud.vert
---------------------------------
  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |struct LightSource {
 12 |  vec4 ambient, diffuse, specular;
 13 |  vec4 positionWorld;
 14 |  vec4 positionEye;
 15 |  vec3 spotDirectionWorld;
 16 |  int directional;
 17 |  vec3 spotDirectionEye;
 18 |  int enabled;
 19 |  float spotExponent, spotCutoff, spotCosCutoff;
 20 |  vec3 attenuation;
 21 |};
 22 |layout (std140, binding=2) uniform Lights {
 23 |  LightSource lights[4];
 24 |};
 25 |layout (std140, binding=1) uniform Material {
 26 |vec4 diffuse;
 27 |vec4 ambient;
 28 |vec4 specular;
 29 |vec4 emissive;
 30 |float shininess;
 31 |int textureCount;
 32 |};
 33 |
 34 |uint numDiffTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 0, 3); }
 35 |uint numSpecTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 3, 3); }
 36 |uint numNormTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 6, 3); }
 37 |uint numHeightTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 9, 3); }
 38 |uint numOpacTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 12, 3); }
 39 |uint numAmbTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 15, 3); }
 40 |
 41 |in vec4 position;
 42 |in vec3 normal;
 43 |
 44 |out vec4 color;
 45 |
 46 |// Suponiendo fuentes puntuales
 47 |vec4 iluminacion(vec3 pos, vec3 N, vec3 V) {
 48 |  // Componente emisiva del material
 49 |  vec4 color = emissive;
 50 |  for (int i = 0; i < lights.length(); i++) {
 51 |    // Si la fuente est apagada, no tenerla en cuenta
 52 |    if (lights[i].enabled == 0)
 53 |      continue;
 54 |
 55 |    // Vector iluminacin (desde vrtice a la fuente)
 56 |    vec3 L = normalize(vec3(lights[i].positionEye) - pos);
 57 |
 58 |    // Multiplicador de la componente difusa
 59 |    float diffuseMult = max(dot(N, L), 0.0);
 60 |    float specularMult = 0.0;
 61 |    if (diffuseMult > 0.0) {
 62 |      // Multiplicador de la componente especular
 63 |      vec3 R = reflect(-L, N);
 64 |      specularMult = max(0.0, dot(R, V));
 65 |      specularMult = pow(specularMult, shininess);
 66 |    }
 67 |
 68 |    float d = distance(pos, vec3(lights[i].positionEye));
 69 |    float kc = lights[i].attenuation.x;
 70 |    float kl = lights[i].attenuation.y;
 71 |    float kq = lights[i].attenuation.z;
 72 |    float attenuation_factor = 1.0/max(1, kc + kl*d + kq*pow(d,2));
 73 |
 74 |    float efecto_foco = 0;
 75 |    float maxLD = max(dot(L, spotDirection), 0);
 76 |    if(spotCutoff == 180){
 77 |        efecto_foco = 1;
 78 |    }
 79 |    else if(maxLD >= spotCosCutoff){
 80 |        efecto_foco = 0;
 81 |    }
 82 |    else{
 83 |        efecto_foco = pow(maxLD, spotExponent);
 84 |    }
 85 |
 86 |    color += attenuation_factor * efecto_foco * 
 87 |            (lights[i].ambient * ambient +
 88 |             lights[i].diffuse * diffuse * diffuseMult +
 89 |             lights[i].specular * specular * specularMult);
 90 |  }
 91 |
 92 |  return color;
 93 |}
 94 |
 95 |void main() {
 96 |  // Normal en el espacio de la cmara
 97 |  vec3 eN = normalize(normalMatrix * normal);
 98 |  // Vrtice en el espacio de la cmara
 99 |  vec3 eposition = vec3(modelviewMatrix * position);
100 |  // Vector vista (desde vrtice a la cmara)
101 |  vec3 V = normalize(-eposition.xyz);
102 |  // Clculo de la iluminacin
103 |  color = iluminacion(eposition, eN, V);
104 |  gl_Position = modelviewprojMatrix * position;
105 |}

Vertex shader: ../p5/gouraud.vert
---------------------------------
  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |struct LightSource {
 12 |  vec4 ambient, diffuse, specular;
 13 |  vec4 positionWorld;
 14 |  vec4 positionEye;
 15 |  vec3 spotDirectionWorld;
 16 |  int directional;
 17 |  vec3 spotDirectionEye;
 18 |  int enabled;
 19 |  float spotExponent, spotCutoff, spotCosCutoff;
 20 |  vec3 attenuation;
 21 |};
 22 |layout (std140, binding=2) uniform Lights {
 23 |  LightSource lights[4];
 24 |};
 25 |layout (std140, binding=1) uniform Material {
 26 |vec4 diffuse;
 27 |vec4 ambient;
 28 |vec4 specular;
 29 |vec4 emissive;
 30 |float shininess;
 31 |int textureCount;
 32 |};
 33 |
 34 |uint numDiffTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 0, 3); }
 35 |uint numSpecTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 3, 3); }
 36 |uint numNormTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 6, 3); }
 37 |uint numHeightTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 9, 3); }
 38 |uint numOpacTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 12, 3); }
 39 |uint numAmbTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 15, 3); }
 40 |
 41 |in vec4 position;
 42 |in vec3 normal;
 43 |
 44 |out vec4 color;
 45 |
 46 |// Suponiendo fuentes puntuales
 47 |vec4 iluminacion(vec3 pos, vec3 N, vec3 V) {
 48 |  // Componente emisiva del material
 49 |  vec4 color = emissive;
 50 |  for (int i = 0; i < lights.length(); i++) {
 51 |    // Si la fuente est apagada, no tenerla en cuenta
 52 |    if (lights[i].enabled == 0)
 53 |      continue;
 54 |
 55 |    // Vector iluminacin (desde vrtice a la fuente)
 56 |    vec3 L = normalize(vec3(lights[i].positionEye) - pos);
 57 |
 58 |    // Multiplicador de la componente difusa
 59 |    float diffuseMult = max(dot(N, L), 0.0);
 60 |    float specularMult = 0.0;
 61 |    if (diffuseMult > 0.0) {
 62 |      // Multiplicador de la componente especular
 63 |      vec3 R = reflect(-L, N);
 64 |      specularMult = max(0.0, dot(R, V));
 65 |      specularMult = pow(specularMult, shininess);
 66 |    }
 67 |
 68 |    float d = distance(pos, vec3(lights[i].positionEye));
 69 |    float kc = lights[i].attenuation.x;
 70 |    float kl = lights[i].attenuation.y;
 71 |    float kq = lights[i].attenuation.z;
 72 |    float attenuation_factor = 1.0/max(1, kc + kl*d + kq*pow(d,2));
 73 |
 74 |    float efecto_foco = 0;
 75 |    float maxLD = max(dot(L, vec3 spotDirectionWorld), 0);
 76 |    if(spotCutoff == 180){
 77 |        efecto_foco = 1;
 78 |    }
 79 |    else if(maxLD >= spotCosCutoff){
 80 |        efecto_foco = 0;
 81 |    }
 82 |    else{
 83 |        efecto_foco = pow(maxLD, spotExponent);
 84 |    }
 85 |
 86 |    color += attenuation_factor * efecto_foco * 
 87 |            (lights[i].ambient * ambient +
 88 |             lights[i].diffuse * diffuse * diffuseMult +
 89 |             lights[i].specular * specular * specularMult);
 90 |  }
 91 |
 92 |  return color;
 93 |}
 94 |
 95 |void main() {
 96 |  // Normal en el espacio de la cmara
 97 |  vec3 eN = normalize(normalMatrix * normal);
 98 |  // Vrtice en el espacio de la cmara
 99 |  vec3 eposition = vec3(modelviewMatrix * position);
100 |  // Vector vista (desde vrtice a la cmara)
101 |  vec3 V = normalize(-eposition.xyz);
102 |  // Clculo de la iluminacin
103 |  color = iluminacion(eposition, eN, V);
104 |  gl_Position = modelviewprojMatrix * position;
105 |}
106 |

Vertex shader: ../p5/gouraud.vert

  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |struct LightSource {
 12 |  vec4 ambient, diffuse, specular;
 13 |  vec4 positionWorld;
 14 |  vec4 positionEye;
 15 |  vec3 spotDirectionWorld;
 16 |  int directional;
 17 |  vec3 spotDirectionEye;
 18 |  int enabled;
 19 |  float spotExponent, spotCutoff, spotCosCutoff;
 20 |  vec3 attenuation;
 21 |};
 22 |layout (std140, binding=2) uniform Lights {
 23 |  LightSource lights[4];
 24 |};
 25 |layout (std140, binding=1) uniform Material {
 26 |vec4 diffuse;
 27 |vec4 ambient;
 28 |vec4 specular;
 29 |vec4 emissive;
 30 |float shininess;
 31 |int textureCount;
 32 |};
 33 |
 34 |uint numDiffTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 0, 3); }
 35 |uint numSpecTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 3, 3); }
 36 |uint numNormTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 6, 3); }
 37 |uint numHeightTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 9, 3); }
 38 |uint numOpacTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 12, 3); }
 39 |uint numAmbTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 15, 3); }
 40 |
 41 |in vec4 position;
 42 |in vec3 normal;
 43 |
 44 |out vec4 color;
 45 |
 46 |// Suponiendo fuentes puntuales
 47 |vec4 iluminacion(vec3 pos, vec3 N, vec3 V) {
 48 |  // Componente emisiva del material
 49 |  vec4 color = emissive;
 50 |  for (int i = 0; i < lights.length(); i++) {
 51 |    // Si la fuente est apagada, no tenerla en cuenta
 52 |    if (lights[i].enabled == 0)
 53 |      continue;
 54 |
 55 |    // Vector iluminacin (desde vrtice a la fuente)
 56 |    vec3 L = normalize(vec3(lights[i].positionEye) - pos);
 57 |
 58 |    // Multiplicador de la componente difusa
 59 |    float diffuseMult = max(dot(N, L), 0.0);
 60 |    float specularMult = 0.0;
 61 |    if (diffuseMult > 0.0) {
 62 |      // Multiplicador de la componente especular
 63 |      vec3 R = reflect(-L, N);
 64 |      specularMult = max(0.0, dot(R, V));
 65 |      specularMult = pow(specularMult, shininess);
 66 |    }
 67 |
 68 |    float d = distance(pos, vec3(lights[i].positionEye));
 69 |    float kc = lights[i].attenuation.x;
 70 |    float kl = lights[i].attenuation.y;
 71 |    float kq = lights[i].attenuation.z;
 72 |    float attenuation_factor = 1.0/max(1, kc + kl*d + kq*pow(d,2));
 73 |
 74 |    float efecto_foco = 0;
 75 |    float maxLD = max(dot(L, spotDirectioEye), 0);
 76 |    if(spotCutoff == 180){
 77 |        efecto_foco = 1;
 78 |    }
 79 |    else if(maxLD >= spotCosCutoff){
 80 |        efecto_foco = 0;
 81 |    }
 82 |    else{
 83 |        efecto_foco = pow(maxLD, spotExponent);
 84 |    }
 85 |
 86 |    color += attenuation_factor * efecto_foco * 
 87 |            (lights[i].ambient * ambient +
 88 |             lights[i].diffuse * diffuse * diffuseMult +
 89 |             lights[i].specular * specular * specularMult);
 90 |  }
 91 |
 92 |  return color;
 93 |}
 94 |
 95 |void main() {
 96 |  // Normal en el espacio de la cmara
 97 |  vec3 eN = normalize(normalMatrix * normal);
 98 |  // Vrtice en el espacio de la cmara
 99 |  vec3 eposition = vec3(modelviewMatrix * position);
100 |  // Vector vista (desde vrtice a la cmara)
101 |  vec3 V = normalize(-eposition.xyz);
102 |  // Clculo de la iluminacin
103 |  color = iluminacion(eposition, eN, V);
104 |  gl_Position = modelviewprojMatrix * position;
105 |}
106 |

[Sun May  1 00:52:43 2022] INF: [shader.cpp (169)] Compilando ../p5/gouraud.vert
[Sun May  1 00:52:43 2022] ERR: [program.cpp (223)] Error compilando el shader:0(56) : error C1503: undefined variable "posicion"
0(57) : error C1503: undefined variable "directional"
0(78) : error C1503: undefined variable "directional"

Vertex shader: ../p5/gouraud.vert
---------------------------------
  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |struct LightSource {
 12 |  vec4 ambient, diffuse, specular;
 13 |  vec4 positionWorld;
 14 |  vec4 positionEye;
 15 |  vec3 spotDirectionWorld;
 16 |  int directional;
 17 |  vec3 spotDirectionEye;
 18 |  int enabled;
 19 |  float spotExponent, spotCutoff, spotCosCutoff;
 20 |  vec3 attenuation;
 21 |};
 22 |layout (std140, binding=2) uniform Lights {
 23 |  LightSource lights[4];
 24 |};
 25 |layout (std140, binding=1) uniform Material {
 26 |vec4 diffuse;
 27 |vec4 ambient;
 28 |vec4 specular;
 29 |vec4 emissive;
 30 |float shininess;
 31 |int textureCount;
 32 |};
 33 |
 34 |uint numDiffTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 0, 3); }
 35 |uint numSpecTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 3, 3); }
 36 |uint numNormTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 6, 3); }
 37 |uint numHeightTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 9, 3); }
 38 |uint numOpacTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 12, 3); }
 39 |uint numAmbTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 15, 3); }
 40 |
 41 |in vec4 position;
 42 |in vec3 normal;
 43 |
 44 |out vec4 color;
 45 |
 46 |// Suponiendo fuentes puntuales
 47 |vec4 iluminacion(vec3 pos, vec3 N, vec3 V) {
 48 |  // Componente emisiva del material
 49 |  vec4 color = emissive;
 50 |  for (int i = 0; i < lights.length(); i++) {
 51 |    // Si la fuente est apagada, no tenerla en cuenta
 52 |    if (lights[i].enabled == 0)
 53 |      continue;
 54 |
 55 |    // Vector iluminacin (desde vrtice a la fuente)
 56 |    vec3 L = normalize(posicion.xyz);
 57 |    if(directional == 0){
 58 |        L = normalize(vec3(lights[i].positionEye) - pos);
 59 |    }
 60 |
 61 |    // Multiplicador de la componente difusa
 62 |    float diffuseMult = max(dot(N, L), 0.0);
 63 |    float specularMult = 0.0;
 64 |    if (diffuseMult > 0.0) {
 65 |      // Multiplicador de la componente especular
 66 |      vec3 R = reflect(-L, N);
 67 |      specularMult = max(0.0, dot(R, V));
 68 |      specularMult = pow(specularMult, shininess);
 69 |    }
 70 |
 71 |    float d = distance(pos, vec3(lights[i].positionEye));
 72 |    float kc = lights[i].attenuation.x;
 73 |    float kl = lights[i].attenuation.y;
 74 |    float kq = lights[i].attenuation.z;
 75 |
 76 |    float attenuation_factor = 1;
 77 |    float efecto_foco = 1;
 78 |    if(directional == 0){
 79 |        attenuation_factor = 1.0/max(1, kc + kl*d + kq*pow(d,2));
 80 |
 81 |        float maxLD = max(dot(-L, lights[i].spotDirectionEye), 0);
 82 |        if(lights[i].spotCutoff == 180){
 83 |            efecto_foco = 1;
 84 |        }
 85 |        else if(maxLD < lights[i].spotCosCutoff){
 86 |            efecto_foco = 0;
 87 |        }
 88 |        else{
 89 |            efecto_foco = pow(maxLD, lights[i].spotExponent);
 90 |        }
 91 |    }   
 92 |
 93 |    color += attenuation_factor * efecto_foco * 
 94 |            (lights[i].ambient * ambient +
 95 |             lights[i].diffuse * diffuse * diffuseMult +
 96 |             lights[i].specular * specular * specularMult);
 97 |  }
 98 |
 99 |  return color;
100 |}
101 |
102 |void main() {
103 |  // Normal en el espacio de la cmara
104 |  vec3 eN = normalize(normalMatrix * normal);
105 |  // Vrtice en el espacio de la cmara
106 |  vec3 eposition = vec3(modelviewMatrix * position);
107 |  // Vector vista (desde vrtice a la cmara)
108 |  vec3 V = normalize(-eposition.xyz);
109 |  // Clculo de la iluminacin
110 |  color = iluminacion(eposition, eN, V);
111 |  gl_Position = modelviewprojMatrix * position;
112 |}
113 |

Vertex shader: ../p5/gouraud.vert
---------------------------------
  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |struct LightSource {
 12 |  vec4 ambient, diffuse, specular;
 13 |  vec4 positionWorld;
 14 |  vec4 positionEye;
 15 |  vec3 spotDirectionWorld;
 16 |  int directional;
 17 |  vec3 spotDirectionEye;
 18 |  int enabled;
 19 |  float spotExponent, spotCutoff, spotCosCutoff;
 20 |  vec3 attenuation;
 21 |};
 22 |layout (std140, binding=2) uniform Lights {
 23 |  LightSource lights[4];
 24 |};
 25 |layout (std140, binding=1) uniform Material {
 26 |vec4 diffuse;
 27 |vec4 ambient;
 28 |vec4 specular;
 29 |vec4 emissive;
 30 |float shininess;
 31 |int textureCount;
 32 |};
 33 |
 34 |uint numDiffTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 0, 3); }
 35 |uint numSpecTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 3, 3); }
 36 |uint numNormTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 6, 3); }
 37 |uint numHeightTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 9, 3); }
 38 |uint numOpacTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 12, 3); }
 39 |uint numAmbTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 15, 3); }
 40 |
 41 |in vec4 position;
 42 |in vec3 normal;
 43 |
 44 |out vec4 color;
 45 |
 46 |// Suponiendo fuentes puntuales
 47 |vec4 iluminacion(vec3 pos, vec3 N, vec3 V) {
 48 |  // Componente emisiva del material
 49 |  vec4 color = emissive;
 50 |  for (int i = 0; i < lights.length(); i++) {
 51 |    // Si la fuente est apagada, no tenerla en cuenta
 52 |    if (lights[i].enabled == 0)
 53 |      continue;
 54 |
 55 |    // Vector iluminacin (desde vrtice a la fuente)
 56 |    vec3 L = normalize(position.xyz);
 57 |    if(directional == 0){
 58 |        L = normalize(vec3(lights[i].positionEye) - pos);
 59 |    }
 60 |
 61 |    // Multiplicador de la componente difusa
 62 |    float diffuseMult = max(dot(N, L), 0.0);
 63 |    float specularMult = 0.0;
 64 |    if (diffuseMult > 0.0) {
 65 |      // Multiplicador de la componente especular
 66 |      vec3 R = reflect(-L, N);
 67 |      specularMult = max(0.0, dot(R, V));
 68 |      specularMult = pow(specularMult, shininess);
 69 |    }
 70 |
 71 |    float d = distance(pos, vec3(lights[i].positionEye));
 72 |    float kc = lights[i].attenuation.x;
 73 |    float kl = lights[i].attenuation.y;
 74 |    float kq = lights[i].attenuation.z;
 75 |
 76 |    float attenuation_factor = 1;
 77 |    float efecto_foco = 1;
 78 |    if(lights[i].directional == 0){
 79 |        attenuation_factor = 1.0/max(1, kc + kl*d + kq*pow(d,2));
 80 |
 81 |        float maxLD = max(dot(-L, lights[i].spotDirectionEye), 0);
 82 |        if(lights[i].spotCutoff == 180){
 83 |            efecto_foco = 1;
 84 |        }
 85 |        else if(maxLD < lights[i].spotCosCutoff){
 86 |            efecto_foco = 0;
 87 |        }
 88 |        else{
 89 |            efecto_foco = pow(maxLD, lights[i].spotExponent);
 90 |        }
 91 |    }   
 92 |
 93 |    color += attenuation_factor * efecto_foco * 
 94 |            (lights[i].ambient * ambient +
 95 |             lights[i].diffuse * diffuse * diffuseMult +
 96 |             lights[i].specular * specular * specularMult);
 97 |  }
 98 |
 99 |  return color;
100 |}
101 |
102 |void main() {
103 |  // Normal en el espacio de la cmara
104 |  vec3 eN = normalize(normalMatrix * normal);
105 |  // Vrtice en el espacio de la cmara
106 |  vec3 eposition = vec3(modelviewMatrix * position);
107 |  // Vector vista (desde vrtice a la cmara)
108 |  vec3 V = normalize(-eposition.xyz);
109 |  // Clculo de la iluminacin
110 |  color = iluminacion(eposition, eN, V);
111 |  gl_Position = modelviewprojMatrix * position;
112 |}
113 |

 23 |  LightSource lights[4];
 24 |};
 25 |layout (std140, binding=1) uniform Material {
 26 |vec4 diffuse;
 27 |vec4 ambient;
 28 |vec4 specular;
 29 |vec4 emissive;
 30 |float shininess;
 31 |int textureCount;
 32 |};
 33 |
 34 |uint numDiffTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 0, 3); }
 35 |uint numSpecTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 3, 3); }
 36 |uint numNormTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 6, 3); }
 37 |uint numHeightTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 9, 3); }
 38 |uint numOpacTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 12, 3); }
 39 |uint numAmbTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 15, 3); }
 40 |
 41 |in vec4 position;
 42 |in vec3 normal;
 43 |
 44 |out vec4 color;
 45 |
 46 |// Suponiendo fuentes puntuales
 47 |vec4 iluminacion(vec3 pos, vec3 N, vec3 V) {
 48 |  // Componente emisiva del material
 49 |  vec4 color = emissive;
 50 |  for (int i = 0; i < lights.length(); i++) {
 51 |    // Si la fuente est apagada, no tenerla en cuenta
 52 |    if (lights[i].enabled == 0)
 53 |      continue;
 54 |
 55 |    // Vector iluminacin (desde vrtice a la fuente)
 56 |    vec3 L = normalize(vec3(lights[i].positionEye);
 57 |    if(lights[i].directional == 0){
 58 |        L = normalize(vec3(lights[i].positionEye) - pos);
 59 |    }
 60 |
 61 |    // Multiplicador de la componente difusa
 62 |    float diffuseMult = max(dot(N, L), 0.0);
 63 |    float specularMult = 0.0;
 64 |    if (diffuseMult > 0.0) {
 65 |      // Multiplicador de la componente especular
 66 |      vec3 R = reflect(-L, N);
 67 |      specularMult = max(0.0, dot(R, V));
 68 |      specularMult = pow(specularMult, shininess);
 69 |    }
 70 |
 71 |    float d = distance(pos, vec3(lights[i].positionEye));
 72 |    float kc = lights[i].attenuation.x;
 73 |    float kl = lights[i].attenuation.y;
 74 |    float kq = lights[i].attenuation.z;
 75 |
 76 |    float attenuation_factor = 1;
 77 |    float efecto_foco = 1;
 78 |    if(lights[i].directional == 0){
 79 |        attenuation_factor = 1.0/max(1, kc + kl*d + kq*pow(d,2));
 80 |
 81 |        float maxLD = max(dot(-L, lights[i].spotDirectionEye), 0);
 82 |        if(lights[i].spotCutoff == 180){
 83 |            efecto_foco = 1;
 84 |        }
 85 |        else if(maxLD < lights[i].spotCosCutoff){
 86 |            efecto_foco = 0;
 87 |        }
 88 |        else{
 89 |            efecto_foco = pow(maxLD, lights[i].spotExponent);
 90 |        }
 91 |    }   
 92 |
 93 |    color += attenuation_factor * efecto_foco * 
 94 |            (lights[i].ambient * ambient +
 95 |             lights[i].diffuse * diffuse * diffuseMult +
 96 |             lights[i].specular * specular * specularMult);
 97 |  }
 98 |
 99 |  return color;
100 |}
101 |
102 |void main() {
103 |  // Normal en el espacio de la cmara
104 |  vec3 eN = normalize(normalMatrix * normal);
105 |  // Vrtice en el espacio de la cmara
106 |  vec3 eposition = vec3(modelviewMatrix * position);
107 |  // Vector vista (desde vrtice a la cmara)
108 |  vec3 V = normalize(-eposition.xyz);
109 |  // Clculo de la iluminacin
110 |  color = iluminacion(eposition, eN, V);
111 |  gl_Position = modelviewprojMatrix * position;
112 |}
113 |

Vertex shader: ../p5/gouraud.vert
---------------------------------
  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |struct LightSource {
 12 |  vec4 ambient, diffuse, specular;
 13 |  vec4 positionWorld;
 14 |  vec4 positionEye;
 15 |  vec3 spotDirectionWorld;
 16 |  int directional;
 17 |  vec3 spotDirectionEye;
 18 |  int enabled;
 19 |  float spotExponent, spotCutoff, spotCosCutoff;
 20 |  vec3 attenuation;
 21 |};
 22 |layout (std140, binding=2) uniform Lights {
 23 |  LightSource lights[4];
 24 |};
 25 |layout (std140, binding=1) uniform Material {
 26 |vec4 diffuse;
 27 |vec4 ambient;
 28 |vec4 specular;
 29 |vec4 emissive;
 30 |float shininess;
 31 |int textureCount;
 32 |};
 33 |
 34 |uint numDiffTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 0, 3); }
 35 |uint numSpecTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 3, 3); }
 36 |uint numNormTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 6, 3); }
 37 |uint numHeightTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 9, 3); }
 38 |uint numOpacTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 12, 3); }
 39 |uint numAmbTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 15, 3); }
 40 |
 41 |in vec4 position;
 42 |in vec3 normal;
 43 |
 44 |out vec4 color;
 45 |
 46 |// Suponiendo fuentes puntuales
 47 |vec4 iluminacion(vec3 pos, vec3 N, vec3 V) {
 48 |  // Componente emisiva del material
 49 |  vec4 color = emissive;
 50 |  for (int i = 0; i < lights.length(); i++) {
 51 |    // Si la fuente est apagada, no tenerla en cuenta
 52 |    if (lights[i].enabled == 0)
 53 |      continue;
 54 |
 55 |    // Vector iluminacin (desde vrtice a la fuente)
 56 |    vec3 L = normalize(vec3(lights[i].positionEye));
 57 |    if(lights[i].directional == 0){
 58 |        L = normalize(vec3(lights[i].positionEye) - pos);
 59 |    }
 60 |
 61 |    // Multiplicador de la componente difusa
 62 |    float diffuseMult = max(dot(N, L), 0.0);
 63 |    float specularMult = 0.0;
 64 |    if (diffuseMult > 0.0) {
 65 |      // Multiplicador de la componente especular
 66 |      vec3 R = reflect(-L, N);
 67 |      specularMult = max(0.0, dot(R, V));
 68 |      specularMult = pow(specularMult, shininess);
 69 |    }
 70 |
 71 |    float d = distance(pos, vec3(lights[i].positionEye));
 72 |    float kc = lights[i].attenuation.x;
 73 |    float kl = lights[i].attenuation.y;
 74 |    float kq = lights[i].attenuation.z;
 75 |
 76 |    float attenuation_factor = 1;
 77 |    float efecto_foco = 1;
 78 |    if(lights[i].directional == 0){
 79 |        attenuation_factor = 1.0/max(1, kc + (kl*d) + (kq*d*d)));
 80 |
 81 |        float maxLD = dot(-L, lights[i].spotDirectionEye);
 82 |        if(lights[i].spotCutoff == 180){
 83 |            efecto_foco = 1;
 84 |        }
 85 |        else if(maxLD < lights[i].spotCosCutoff){
 86 |            efecto_foco = 0;
 87 |        }
 88 |        else{
 89 |            efecto_foco = pow(maxLD, lights[i].spotExponent);
 90 |        }
 91 |    }   
 92 |
 93 |    color += attenuation_factor * efecto_foco * 
 94 |            (lights[i].ambient * ambient +
 95 |             lights[i].diffuse * diffuse * diffuseMult +
 96 |             lights[i].specular * specular * specularMult);
 97 |  }
 98 |
 99 |  return color;
100 |}
101 |
102 |void main() {
103 |  // Normal en el espacio de la cmara
104 |  vec3 eN = normalize(normalMatrix * normal);
105 |  // Vrtice en el espacio de la cmara
106 |  vec3 eposition = vec3(modelviewMatrix * position);
107 |  // Vector vista (desde vrtice a la cmara)
108 |  vec3 V = normalize(-eposition.xyz);
109 |  // Clculo de la iluminacin
110 |  color = iluminacion(eposition, eN, V);
111 |  gl_Position = modelviewprojMatrix * position;
112 |}
113 |

Vertex shader: ../p5/gouraud.vert
---------------------------------
  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |struct LightSource {
 12 |  vec4 ambient, diffuse, specular;
 13 |  vec4 positionWorld;
 14 |  vec4 positionEye;
 15 |  vec3 spotDirectionWorld;
 16 |  int directional;
 17 |  vec3 spotDirectionEye;
 18 |  int enabled;
 19 |  float spotExponent, spotCutoff, spotCosCutoff;
 20 |  vec3 attenuation;
 21 |};
 22 |layout (std140, binding=2) uniform Lights {
 23 |  LightSource lights[4];
 24 |};
 25 |layout (std140, binding=1) uniform Material {
 26 |vec4 diffuse;
 27 |vec4 ambient;
 28 |vec4 specular;
 29 |vec4 emissive;
 30 |float shininess;
 31 |int textureCount;
 32 |};
 33 |
 34 |uint numDiffTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 0, 3); }
 35 |uint numSpecTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 3, 3); }
 36 |uint numNormTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 6, 3); }
 37 |uint numHeightTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 9, 3); }
 38 |uint numOpacTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 12, 3); }
 39 |uint numAmbTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 15, 3); }
 40 |
 41 |in vec4 position;
 42 |in vec3 normal;
 43 |
 44 |out vec4 color;
 45 |
 46 |// Suponiendo fuentes puntuales
 47 |vec4 iluminacion(vec3 pos, vec3 N, vec3 V) {
 48 |  // Componente emisiva del material
 49 |  vec4 color = emissive;
 50 |  for (int i = 0; i < lights.length(); i++) {
 51 |    // Si la fuente est apagada, no tenerla en cuenta
 52 |    if (lights[i].enabled == 0)
 53 |      continue;
 54 |
 55 |    // Vector iluminacin (desde vrtice a la fuente)
 56 |    vec3 L = normalize(vec3(lights[i].positionEye));
 57 |    if(lights[i].directional == 0){
 58 |        L = normalize(vec3(lights[i].positionEye) - pos);
 59 |    }
 60 |
 61 |    // Multiplicador de la componente difusa
 62 |    float diffuseMult = max(dot(N, L), 0.0);
 63 |    float specularMult = 0.0;
 64 |    if (diffuseMult > 0.0) {
 65 |      // Multiplicador de la componente especular
 66 |      vec3 R = reflect(-L, N);
 67 |      specularMult = max(0.0, dot(R, V));
 68 |      specularMult = pow(specularMult, shininess);
 69 |    }
 70 |
 71 |    float d = distance(pos, vec3(lights[i].positionEye));
 72 |    float kc = lights[i].attenuation.x;
 73 |    float kl = lights[i].attenuation.y;
 74 |    float kq = lights[i].attenuation.z;
 75 |
 76 |    float attenuation_factor = 1;
 77 |    float efecto_foco = 1;
 78 |    if(lights[i].directional == 0){
 79 |        attenuation_factor = 1.0/max(1, kc + (kl*d) + (kq*d*d)));
 80 |
 81 |        float maxLD = max(dot(-L, lights[i].spotDirectionEye), 0);
 82 |        if(lights[i].spotCutoff == 180){
 83 |            efecto_foco = 1;
 84 |        }
 85 |        else if(maxLD < lights[i].spotCosCutoff){
 86 |            efecto_foco = 0;
 87 |        }
 88 |        else{
 89 |            efecto_foco = pow(maxLD, lights[i].spotExponent);
 90 |        }
 91 |    }   
 92 |
 93 |    color += attenuation_factor * efecto_foco * 
 94 |            (lights[i].ambient * ambient +
 95 |             lights[i].diffuse * diffuse * diffuseMult +
 96 |             lights[i].specular * specular * specularMult);
 97 |  }
 98 |
 99 |  return color;
100 |}
101 |
102 |void main() {
103 |  // Normal en el espacio de la cmara
104 |  vec3 eN = normalize(normalMatrix * normal);
105 |  // Vrtice en el espacio de la cmara
106 |  vec3 eposition = vec3(modelviewMatrix * position);
107 |  // Vector vista (desde vrtice a la cmara)
108 |  vec3 V = normalize(-eposition.xyz);
109 |  // Clculo de la iluminacin
110 |  color = iluminacion(eposition, eN, V);
111 |  gl_Position = modelviewprojMatrix * position;
112 |}
113 |

[Sun May  1 02:29:23 2022] ERR: [program.cpp (223)] Error compilando el shader:0(105) : error C7011: implicit cast from "vec4" to "vec3"
0(105) : error C7011: implicit cast from "vec4" to "vec3"

Fragment shader: ../p5/phong.frag
---------------------------------
  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |struct LightSource {
 12 |  vec4 ambient, diffuse, specular;
 13 |  vec4 positionWorld;
 14 |  vec4 positionEye;
 15 |  vec3 spotDirectionWorld;
 16 |  int directional;
 17 |  vec3 spotDirectionEye;
 18 |  int enabled;
 19 |  float spotExponent, spotCutoff, spotCosCutoff;
 20 |  vec3 attenuation;
 21 |};
 22 |layout (std140, binding=2) uniform Lights {
 23 |  LightSource lights[4];
 24 |};
 25 |layout (std140, binding=1) uniform Material {
 26 |vec4 diffuse;
 27 |vec4 ambient;
 28 |vec4 specular;
 29 |vec4 emissive;
 30 |float shininess;
 31 |int textureCount;
 32 |};
 33 |
 34 |uint numDiffTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 0, 3); }
 35 |uint numSpecTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 3, 3); }
 36 |uint numNormTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 6, 3); }
 37 |uint numHeightTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 9, 3); }
 38 |uint numOpacTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 12, 3); }
 39 |uint numAmbTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 15, 3); }
 40 |
 41 |in vec4 eposition;
 42 |in vec4 enormal;
 43 |
 44 |out vec4 fragColor;
 45 |
 46 |// Suponiendo fuentes puntuales
 47 |vec4 iluminacion(vec3 pos, vec3 N, vec3 V) {
 48 |  // Componente emisiva del material
 49 |  vec4 color = emissive;
 50 |  for (int i = 0; i < lights.length(); i++) {
 51 |    // Si la fuente est apagada, no tenerla en cuenta
 52 |    if (lights[i].enabled == 0)
 53 |      continue;
 54 |
 55 |    // Vector iluminacin (desde vrtice a la fuente)
 56 |    vec3 L = normalize(vec3(lights[i].positionEye));
 57 |    if(lights[i].directional == 0){
 58 |        L = normalize(vec3(lights[i].positionEye) - pos);
 59 |    }
 60 |
 61 |    // Multiplicador de la componente difusa
 62 |    float diffuseMult = max(dot(N, L), 0.0);
 63 |    float specularMult = 0.0;
 64 |    if (diffuseMult > 0.0) {
 65 |      // Multiplicador de la componente especular
 66 |      vec3 R = reflect(-L, N);
 67 |      specularMult = max(0.0, dot(R, V));
 68 |      specularMult = pow(specularMult, shininess);
 69 |    }
 70 |
 71 |    float d = distance(pos, vec3(lights[i].positionEye));
 72 |    float kc = lights[i].attenuation.x;
 73 |    float kl = lights[i].attenuation.y;
 74 |    float kq = lights[i].attenuation.z;
 75 |
 76 |    float attenuation_factor = 1;
 77 |    float efecto_foco = 1;
 78 |    if(lights[i].directional == 0){
 79 |        attenuation_factor = 1.0/max(1, kc + (kl*d) + (kq*d*d));
 80 |
 81 |        float maxLD = max(dot(-L, lights[i].spotDirectionEye), 0);
 82 |        if(lights[i].spotCutoff == 180){
 83 |            efecto_foco = 1;
 84 |        }
 85 |        else if(maxLD < lights[i].spotCosCutoff){
 86 |            efecto_foco = 0;
 87 |        }
 88 |        else{
 89 |            efecto_foco = pow(maxLD, lights[i].spotExponent);
 90 |        }
 91 |    }   
 92 |
 93 |    color += attenuation_factor * efecto_foco * 
 94 |            (lights[i].ambient * ambient +
 95 |             lights[i].diffuse * diffuse * diffuseMult +
 96 |             lights[i].specular * specular * specularMult);
 97 |  }
 98 |
 99 |  return color;
100 |}
101 |
102 |void main() {

Fragment shader: ../p5/phong.frag
---------------------------------
  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |
  4 |in vec3 eposition;
  5 |in vec3 enormal;
  6 |
  7 |out vec4 fragColor;
  8 |
  9 |// Suponiendo fuentes puntuales
 10 |vec4 iluminacion(vec3 pos, vec3 N, vec3 V) {
 11 |  // Componente emisiva del material
 12 |  vec4 color = emissive;
 13 |  for (int i = 0; i < lights.length(); i++) {
 14 |    // Si la fuente est apagada, no tenerla en cuenta
 15 |    if (lights[i].enabled == 0)
 16 |      continue;
 17 |
 18 |    // Vector iluminacin (desde vrtice a la fuente)
 19 |    vec3 L = normalize(vec3(lights[i].positionEye));
 20 |    if(lights[i].directional == 0){
 21 |        L = normalize(vec3(lights[i].positionEye) - pos);
 22 |    }
 23 |
 24 |    // Multiplicador de la componente difusa
 25 |    float diffuseMult = max(dot(N, L), 0.0);
 26 |    float specularMult = 0.0;
 27 |    if (diffuseMult > 0.0) {
 28 |      // Multiplicador de la componente especular
 29 |      vec3 R = reflect(-L, N);
 30 |      specularMult = max(0.0, dot(R, V));
 31 |      specularMult = pow(specularMult, shininess);
 32 |    }
 33 |
 34 |    float d = distance(pos, vec3(lights[i].positionEye));
 35 |    float kc = lights[i].attenuation.x;
 36 |    float kl = lights[i].attenuation.y;
 37 |    float kq = lights[i].attenuation.z;
 38 |
 39 |    float attenuation_factor = 1;
 40 |    float efecto_foco = 1;
 41 |    if(lights[i].directional == 0){
 42 |        attenuation_factor = 1.0/max(1, kc + (kl*d) + (kq*d*d));
 43 |
 44 |        float maxLD = max(dot(-L, lights[i].spotDirectionEye), 0);
 45 |        if(lights[i].spotCutoff == 180){
 46 |            efecto_foco = 1;
 47 |        }
 48 |        else if(maxLD < lights[i].spotCosCutoff){
 49 |            efecto_foco = 0;
 50 |        }
 51 |        else{
 52 |            efecto_foco = pow(maxLD, lights[i].spotExponent);
 53 |        }
 54 |    }   
 55 |
 56 |    color += attenuation_factor * efecto_foco * 
 57 |            (lights[i].ambient * ambient +
 58 |             lights[i].diffuse * diffuse * diffuseMult +
 59 |             lights[i].specular * specular * specularMult);
 60 |  }
 61 |
 62 |  return color;
 63 |}
 64 |
 65 |void main() {
 66 |  vec3 V = normalize(-eposition.xyz);
 67 |  // Clculo de la iluminacin
 68 |  fragColor = iluminacion(eposition, enormal, V);
 69 |}
 70 |

Fragment shader: ../p5/phong.frag
---------------------------------
  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |struct LightSource {
  4 |  vec4 ambient, diffuse, specular;
  5 |  vec4 positionWorld;
  6 |  vec4 positionEye;
  7 |  vec3 spotDirectionWorld;
  8 |  int directional;
  9 |  vec3 spotDirectionEye;
 10 |  int enabled;
 11 |  float spotExponent, spotCutoff, spotCosCutoff;
 12 |  vec3 attenuation;
 13 |};
 14 |layout (std140, binding=2) uniform Lights {
 15 |  LightSource lights[4];
 16 |};
 17 |layout (std140, binding=1) uniform Material {
 18 |vec4 diffuse;
 19 |vec4 ambient;
 20 |vec4 specular;
 21 |vec4 emissive;
 22 |float shininess;
 23 |int textureCount;
 24 |};
 25 |
 26 |uint numDiffTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 0, 3); }
 27 |uint numSpecTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 3, 3); }
 28 |uint numNormTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 6, 3); }
 29 |uint numHeightTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 9, 3); }
 30 |uint numOpacTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 12, 3); }
 31 |uint numAmbTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 15, 3); }
 32 |
 33 |in vec3 eposition;
 34 |in vec3 enormal;
 35 |
 36 |out vec4 fragColor;
 37 |
 38 |// Suponiendo fuentes puntuales
 39 |vec4 iluminacion(vec3 pos, vec3 N, vec3 V) {
 40 |  // Componente emisiva del material
 41 |  vec4 color = emissive;
 42 |  for (int i = 0; i < lights.length(); i++) {
 43 |    // Si la fuente est apagada, no tenerla en cuenta
 44 |    if (lights[i].enabled == 0)
 45 |      continue;
 46 |
 47 |    // Vector iluminacin (desde vrtice a la fuente)
 48 |    vec3 L = normalize(vec3(lights[i].positionEye));
 49 |    if(lights[i].directional == 0){
 50 |        L = normalize(vec3(lights[i].positionEye) - pos);
 51 |    }
 52 |
 53 |    // Multiplicador de la componente difusa
 54 |    float diffuseMult = max(dot(N, L), 0.0);
 55 |    float specularMult = 0.0;
 56 |    if (diffuseMult > 0.0) {
 57 |      // Multiplicador de la componente especular
 58 |      vec3 R = reflect(-L, N);
 59 |      specularMult = max(0.0, dot(R, V));
 60 |      specularMult = pow(specularMult, shininess);
 61 |    }
 62 |
 63 |    float d = distance(pos, vec3(lights[i].positionEye));
 64 |    float kc = lights[i].attenuation.x;
 65 |    float kl = lights[i].attenuation.y;
 66 |    float kq = lights[i].attenuation.z;
 67 |
 68 |    float attenuation_factor = 1;
 69 |    float efecto_foco = 1;
 70 |    if(lights[i].directional == 0){
 71 |        attenuation_factor = 1.0/max(1, kc + (kl*d) + (kq*d*d));
 72 |
 73 |        float maxLD = max(dot(-L, lights[i].spotDirectionEye), 0);
 74 |        if(lights[i].spotCutoff == 180){
 75 |            efecto_foco = 1;
 76 |        }
 77 |        else if(maxLD < lights[i].spotCosCutoff){
 78 |            efecto_foco = 0;
 79 |        }
 80 |        else{
 81 |            efecto_foco = pow(maxLD, lights[i].spotExponent);
 82 |        }
 83 |    }   
 84 |
 85 |    color += attenuation_factor * efecto_foco * 
 86 |            (lights[i].ambient * ambient +
 87 |             lights[i].diffuse * diffuse * diffuseMult +
 88 |             lights[i].specular * specular * specularMult);
 89 |  }
 90 |
 91 |  return color;
 92 |}
 93 |
 94 |void main() {
 95 |  enormal = normalize(enormal);
 96 |  vec3 V = normalize(-eposition.xyz);
 97 |  // Clculo de la iluminacin
 98 |  fragColor = iluminacion(eposition, enormal, V);
 99 |}

---------------------------------
  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |struct LightSource {
  4 |  vec4 ambient, diffuse, specular;
  5 |  vec4 positionWorld;
  6 |  vec4 positionEye;
  7 |  vec3 spotDirectionWorld;
  8 |  int directional;
  9 |  vec3 spotDirectionEye;
 10 |  int enabled;
 11 |  float spotExponent, spotCutoff, spotCosCutoff;
 12 |  vec3 attenuation;
 13 |};
 14 |layout (std140, binding=2) uniform Lights {
 15 |  LightSource lights[4];
 16 |};
 17 |layout (std140, binding=1) uniform Material {
 18 |vec4 diffuse;
 19 |vec4 ambient;
 20 |vec4 specular;
 21 |vec4 emissive;
 22 |float shininess;
 23 |int textureCount;
 24 |};
 25 |
 26 |uint numDiffTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 0, 3); }
 27 |uint numSpecTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 3, 3); }
 28 |uint numNormTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 6, 3); }
 29 |uint numHeightTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 9, 3); }
 30 |uint numOpacTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 12, 3); }
 31 |uint numAmbTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 15, 3); }
 32 |
 33 |in vec3 eposition;
 34 |in vec3 enormal;
 35 |
 36 |out vec4 fragColor;
 37 |
 38 |vec4 iluminacion(vec3 pos, vec3 N, vec3 V) {
 39 |  // Componente emisiva del material
 40 |  vec4 color = emissive;
 41 |
 42 |  for (int i = 0; i < lights.length(); i++) {
 43 |    // Si la fuente est apagada, no tenerla en cuenta
 44 |    if (lights[i].enabled == 0)
 45 |      continue;
 46 |
 47 |    // Vector iluminacin en fuente direccional
 48 |    vec3 L = normalize(vec3(lights[i].positionEye));
 49 |    if(lights[i].directional == 0){
 50 |        // Vector iluminacin (desde vrtice a la fuente)
 51 |        L = normalize(vec3(lights[i].positionEye) - pos);
 52 |    }
 53 |
 54 |    // Multiplicador de la componente difusa
 55 |    float diffuseMult = max(dot(N, L), 0.0);
 56 |    float specularMult = 0.0;
 57 |    if (diffuseMult > 0.0) {
 58 |      // Multiplicador de la componente especular
 59 |      vec3 R = reflect(-L, N);
 60 |      specularMult = max(0.0, dot(R, V));
 61 |      specularMult = pow(specularMult, shininess);
 62 |    }
 63 |
 64 |    float d = distance(pos, vec3(lights[i].positionEye));
 65 |    float kc = lights[i].attenuation.x;
 66 |    float kl = lights[i].attenuation.y;
 67 |    float kq = lights[i].attenuation.z;
 68 |
 69 |    float attenuation_factor = 1;
 70 |    float focus_effect = 1;
 71 |    if(lights[i].directional == 0){
 72 |        // Factor de atenuacion para luz no direccional
 73 |        attenuation_factor = 1.0/max(1, kc + (kl*d) + (kq*d*d));
 74 |
 75 |        float maxLD = max(dot(-L, lights[i].spotDirectionEye), 0);
 76 |        // Efecto foco para luz no direccional
 77 |        if(lights[i].spotCutoff == 180){
 78 |            focus_effect = 1;
 79 |        }
 80 |        else if(maxLD < lights[i].spotCosCutoff){
 81 |            focus_effect = 0;
 82 |        }
 83 |        else{
 84 |            focus_effect = pow(maxLD, lights[i].spotExponent);
 85 |        }
 86 |    }   
 87 |
 88 |    color += attenuation_factor * efecto_foco * 
 89 |            (lights[i].ambient * ambient +
 90 |             lights[i].diffuse * diffuse * diffuseMult +
 91 |             lights[i].specular * specular * specularMult);
 92 |  }
 93 |
 94 |  return color;
 95 |}
 96 |
 97 |void main() {
 98 |  vec3 nenormal = normalize(enormal);
 99 |  vec3 V = normalize(-eposition.xyz);
100 |  // Clculo de la iluminacin
101 |  fragColor = iluminacion(eposition, nenormal, V);
102 |}
